Jooɗiiɗo Kirchner o seedini niyaamu makko ngam yahugo ngam ardiiɗo leydi nder Argentine Theatre, wuro ngoɗngol o huutori ngam fuɗɗugo fedde makko e 2005 ngam senatoore bana membaajo fedde Buenos Aires.
Jaɓɓorgal ngal ummii sabu ceede ɗe njettinaama ngam wallitde e ummitaade ɓaawo henndu Katrina; ko woɓɓe e jaɓɓeeɓe ceede naniiɗe ceeɗaani wi'i "Deftere Orleans Hesre Bush."
Ndee miijooji jaatiido e dow golle fayyinde caggal halkere, tigi-tiggi ko haala no mbeltidiinde golleeji fayyinde ɗum teeŋti e yimɓe ganndo'en Washington.
Yimɓe ɓurɓe miliyanji nayi njahi Roma ngam arde janaja.
Yimɓe nguurndam ɓee ɗuuɗi no feewi haa fow fuu waawaay naatde janajaaje nder saare Peter's.

Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Aggooje Agg
Nder hitaande 1956, Słania o yahii leydi Suwede, to nder duuɓi tati ɓaawo, o fuɗɗi golle e jaŋde postal Suwede, o laati ardiiɗo mooftoowo suura maɓɓe.
O wurtini timminannde teemeddere (1,000) keese baande Suwedan e leydeeki goɗɗe cappanɗe tati (28).
Nguurndam golle makko no woodi daraja e fooli ɗum no feewi haa o gooto e seeda "ino anndaa" hakkunde yimɓe njaggitooɓe stampuuji. Woɓɓe no heeranii njaggaago golle makko tan.
Tambeere makko teemerre cappande jeetati nden woni "Golleeji Mawɗi ɗi Laamɓe Suweed en Goolli" ɗi David Klöcker Ehrenstrahl waɗi hitaande 2000, ɗum ko winndaaɗum nder Deftere Guinness ɗen.
O woni kadi e golle timmingol ceede ngolɗe ngam leyɗe keewɗe, misaluji ɓaawo ɗoo e golle makko ko misaluji jaŋde ardiiɓe leydi (Prime Ministerial portraits) e yeeso ceede Kanada kesi $5 e $100.
Ɓaawo balleeji ngari, Gibson neltinaama asibiti amma o maayi ɓaawo seeɗa.
**Pullo jippordo mota, mo duuɓi mum ɗuuɓi capanɗe joweeyi e nayi, alaa ko o weeɗii nder baabal ngal.**

Daraja mum rokkiti nder karnuwol joweetatiyo sabu hujja wonde konu crusader en ngartiri e bee baaruuji bana alhariri e remme boɗeeje ɗe keɓaaɗe teddungal ɓuri jawdi suuqji Byzantine nastaano.
Ko e nder wakkati on nden de ardungal galluure koltiroore daga Constantinople haa Paris woni.
Nder labiirki gootel, batte gotik ngartiri hakkunde karnuwol sappow e go'o e sappow e ɗiɗi e karnuwol sappow e nayi.
Fombina fuɗɗoode, comci ɗon njogake barke mawɗo daga aada Byzantine to fuɗirde hirnaange.
Kono, sabu laaɓal njamndi habaru, nootol e hirnaange waawan waɗugo ɓaawo duuɓi 25 haa 30.
Ha fuɗɗoode saare hakkunde, hirnaange Yuruba fuɗɗi hollitaade mballa mum. Go'o nder mawɗe ɓesdital nder jamani on sabu konuuji safaliiɓe, yimɓe fuɗɗi huutoraade buttonji ngam tabbitaade comci.
Ndaaɗi ngesa ko ngesa nde aɗi waɗetee ngam a reentina nyaamdu haa heewta bukata gorko/debbo ngesɗo e ɓeynguure mum tan.
Ngeendam ngesa ko laabi ngesa pamarimmari, lollitol, ko kadi ngesa jemma ngesa, bee seediji ngesaaji jogorɗi e leydi ndin e wakkati ngesa, bee juude ngesa bee laabi pamari ngam ɓeydude njamndi.
Yimɓe remooɓe ɓurɓe luttuɗe, ko nder remo nguurndam tan ɓe ngoni, e jonta non kanko woni haala nder lesdiije jamfaaji keewɗi.
Kooltuuraaji pamaraaji ngardinta yimɓe wonɓe miijooji go'o ɓe, ɓe nanngaama ɓe wooraama e ɗa'eede jaamu'aaji renndo, ndeke ɗum naffa ɓe ngam ɓe keeru darnde mum en.
Golleeji pamarii ngoni keeriiɗi sabu duuɓi, leƴƴi, nguurndam, nokkuure, e/bee rewɓe memba'en.
Ngoniiji ɗe keeritol golle fedde janngirde bana keeritol ngol, limngal ɗemngal, jamdi hollo, diina, siyasaji, hakkiilo rewɓe e worɓe, nokkuuje leydi, ko hawri ko ɗuuɗi.
Yimɓe fedde wootere nder renndo lollinirteeɗe limgal maɓɓe e nder renndo ɗuum bee huutoreeje keewɗe ceede e tinndi kuuje cosɗe, ɗum naati cosɗe-ndiyam, tabiyeeji, e ɗemɗe keeriiɗe.
Gootal e laabi ɓurɗi heewde ngam hollitde barke jaŋde e jama'aare, ko jogoraade misalaaji tawi ɓiɓɓe pamareeɓe, sabu hersinde, ko toñe, ko yoɓɓitaare, ɓe jaŋtaaka e jama'aare e mawɓe nde ɓe mawni.
Nderɓe ɓee no wi'ee "feral" maa deƴƴe. Woɓɓe nderɓe deƴƴe ɓee, yimɓe (looƴtiiɗo no maɓɓe baaba'en maa yumma'en) no ndokka nder suudu; nder woɓɓe koɗɗe, accitgol nderɗe ɗee ko sabu ɓe baaba'en maa yumma'en coɓɓa nderɗe ɗee sabu haqqilla maa ɓandu muuɗum na'i.
Walaaɓe sukaaɓe daanyaaɓe nder ladde, ɓe ngoni mbaɗi haalaaji kalluɗi walla ɗukkundi pamare ngam ɓe accu ko ɓe doggi.
Woɓɓe wi'etee ɗum ko dabbaaji ngardi ɓe; woɓɓe non wi'etee ɗum ko ɓe nguurii ladde tokko ɓe.
Nde cukalel poolal nguurndam mum fow ina woodi nguurndam jawdi bee himbe, cukalel ngel holla dabi'uuji (ha der keeriiji cellal mum) ko famdaani bana dabi'uuji jawdi ngel nder nguurndam, bana huluki mum bee daggaaki mum bee himbe.
Nde njande lesdi ɗum kuugal (project-based learning) waawi jaɓɓude ko jannde ɓuri newude e ɓuri welɗude, wallitaare (scaffolding) yahata yeeso ɗuum.
Jaɓɓarde wonaa laawol jannde, ammaa wallaango ngal wallitata yimɓe ɓe ngoni e jannde kesere bana huutoraade porogaram komputa keso walla fuɗɗaade golle kese.
Keewɗe mbaawi won'de ko e internet e ko laatoo, faamude, jannginoowo ko fannu keewa, amma non boo ko o munyeejo pepaajo pamaro nder Microsoft Office.
Ndaareeki cuuɗi nder software ɗen, ko ngam lannginaade, nannginaade, e faanditaade golle ɗe nguurndam jannginoowo heewi haɗtaade waɗugo hoore mum.
Ɓiɓɓe ndenndinaama nder galleeji reenaaɓe sabu dalillaaji keewɗi, gila e heedhere, haa e ɗikkital, haa kadi e gulle.
Hay cukalel gootel wanaa sadde ɓamtaade e nokkuure nde wonaa ndiyamɗum, ndimɗum e jannde, ammaa ɓe mbaɗata.
ٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰٰ We perceive the Foster Care System to be a safety zone for these children. . Amina, muna kallon tsarin kula da yara kanana a matsayin wuri mai aminci ga wadannan yaran.
**Fedde renndo amen fa'a wallitagol e reende ko seeda haa ɗe ngabba galleeji celluɗi, reendeeki bee yiɗde, jannde tabbitunde, e reendeeki cellal bee barke.**
Ndeenki reenirde ina jogii himmeeje no o mofta kala ko homeeji maɓɓe ɓe nguurondiri ɓe ngalaaano.
Internet ɗon hawrita ɓannduuje jaŋde e hakkunde jama'a e jaŋde hakkunde yimɓe.
Ngurndan cemtinɗe ইন্টারনেট ngoni dalilai jogiiɗe fa'iidaaji e no nguurndam fa'ida e nange.
Woni misal, "andannde" e "dentinal" ko andaaɗe ko sababuuji teeɗɗiɗi ngam huutoraade Internet (James e takkoreeji, 1995).
"Fattaaki hoore" e "darde jokkondiral" kadi Eighmey e McCord (1998) ngi'i ɗum en bana laabi haayre kesi nde yimɓe keɓata nde ɓe nyoorti internet.
Ndaareeki e kuugal windugo bidiyo nastini gandal mawngal nder fasiruki yeesooji pamaraji, ciirɗi yeeso ngondiɗi seeɗa nder teemerre sekunde.
Ko andi, ɓe mbi'i a waawi anndude to neɗɗo seŋti, to a faaminii miijooji pamari no feewi.
Oliver Sacks, nder pepol makko wi'eteeɗo "Haala Laamɗo," o holli no yimɓe ɓe ngonaa waawɓe faamude haala sabu hallallaaji nder ɓernde, kadi kamɓe ina mbaawi anndude goonga-joonde haqqiika.
O wi'i non kanko, oɗon miila, semmbe értugo mbeɗaaɗi ɗanndaɗi himɓe ina waawi wonde e nguurndam keeriiɗam bee dabbaaji ɗe kaayeeji boɗeeji.
Ndidɗiireeki winndere hitande cappanɗe ɗiɗi nden hollii wonde ummatoore jiineeji ina woodi ɗiɗi: ummatoore suuɗitiriinde e ummatoore bayyiniinde.
Ceerno wallifa taƴre geneetik keesum, gamdi cuɓal naayi ɗum daga caangal wallifaaji kollitaaɗi.
Ceernungal e jogitaggal ngoni lortinaaji keerol caggal e yeeso hakkunde luumooji didi nder jamaanu kala.
Haa boodeeri, ɗum te'iɗi ngam billaamaajo mo nguurndam reedu mum famɗi e neɗɗo, ngam haɓɓita haaje mum e geƴeeniiji amino daga ma'aji leɗɗe ɗi ngoni.
Ko tottaa ɗum, ɗum naati e hakke mawɗe: reedu walaa, nyaamdu bonii, e nde tawii ɗum timmi maayde.
Ngeendam leɗɗe ɓurde newi lelnugo ko proteinaji ɗi ngoni nder dowre e legumji, ammaa ɗumɗon ɗuuɗi mettugo haa primateeji wakkati amin ngonaa ɗum dafinaa.
Ammaa kadi, nyaamduuji diyam (boorooje, tuppule, bee'i) tan wonaa ko newii yo yoora, amma hi'aaddini proteinji keewɗi ɗi ngoodi amino asidiiji pawɗi.
Ko ɗume fuu e nder miijo, wanaa haaɗi maa men haaɓɓa maama'en amen ɓee ngoodaa laawol feere ngam faabooɗe "caayeeje protein" maɓɓe bana no cimpanseeji nder ladde savana faabooɗirta jooni.
Taaskina ɗaandi ko feere yuurnitagol e lokkitiɗaandu nder ɗaande ma aadaaŋge, hade ma a hootu ɗaande ɓaawo wakkati pamarun (mintinaaji 10-60).
Ɗum nootii teeŋteeŋ e kuutortooɗe alarmoore ɗemngal ngam a waylito e miijo maa nder alhaali ko a hallaataa.
Si a tawii hooreejo maa na yoola horloge nder ɗaandu maa, a waawi a waɗa ɗum gesiɗe feccere suudu ndu, ɗum na fewja ma a ummo daga ɗaandu ngam mumtee ɗum.

Ɗum en miijooji kollitaa yimɓe na'i bu'aatuuji e/ko yidde teeɓiiɗe nder pittaali maɓɓe nde ɓe mawni haa ɓe ngoni mawniraaɓe.
Ɗum en miijooji no yimɓe woɗɓe njiɗiri huunde, e ko woni e nokkuure maɓɓe foolata ɓe ngoola huunde walla ɓe ngoolataa.
Teoriyaaji labgal golle ɗiɗi ɗe keewi limteeɗe ko Teoriya Darajaaji Mawnitaare Maslow e kadi Teoriya Bakteeruje Ɗiɗi Hertzberg.
Aɗan ko ɗum woni, jikkuuji ɗiɗi potti feeñde nde ardiiɓe fuɗɗi ardude yimɓe ɓe gollinoo e maɓɓe. Fuɗɗorde gootel ndee ko ɓe ceertiinde ko nde ɓe nelaaɗi e "gooto e sukaaɓe" (ko rewɓe).
Ndenndaagu gardiiɗo ngoo no heɓa caɗeele nder waɗugo miijooji ɗi nelaaɓe nani'aa, e golle jeertol, e ɗaartol golle, e newnugo golle, e nanngugo yimɓe ngam golle maɓɓe.
To bange goɗɗo, neɗɗo fuɗɗoto hulɓinaade haa o waɗi hoore mum neɗɗo mo alaa andal, mo nuŋŋi wonde ko o waylita kala ko fedde ndee eɓe ngalaa e mum, o waɗa dum ko hoore mum.
Ko ɗum woni, ardiiɗo moƴƴi, ko o jogii hakke waɗugo golle jaɓde e waɗugo golle bangeeje ɗe fedde nden.
Ɗumtagal ngal, lindi, ko ɗum waɗata faandu hakkunde ardiiɓe e jeyaaɓe fedde ndee.
Kuugal e fedde internetire ɗum ko ɗaɗɗi ɗum e mbaydi, bana kuugal e fedde kaaldungal, amma woodi tawi feccere pamare.
Yimɓe e fedde golle nder internet, ɓe ɗuuɗi, ɓe ngoni ko hakkunde yimɓe ɓe poti golla e maɓɓe.
**Maa ɓe ɗuuɗi laamu hoore maɓɓe ɓuri feddeeji goɗɗi sabu feddeeji maɓɓe ina kawra dow sa'aaji keeriɗi, ɗum waawataa faamaade e jaagorɓe gure maɓɓe.**
Wondiirde "fedde moƴƴere nde wonaa fooɗunteende" (Larson e LaFasto, 1989, p109) kadi ko fedde keeriiɗe nder fedde gollooɓe nder internet.
"Fedde "ɓurnde suuɗaade" woni fedde jaagorɗe nde gooto e gooto e memba'en nattere. Fedde ɓurnde suuɗaade ɗon tagga miijaaje (jaangoole) ngam gooto e gooto e memba."
Haa koɗal jaŋde fedde nani yiɗi yahugo nder kuugal ɗuuɗungal waktu ngam wallugo fedde jaŋde? Go'o daliila ngam jaggugo miijooji jaŋde fedde nder golle ko waylugo.
Nde ngongaaji denndaangal mari nofaatirde, ɗe gollitirtee no moƴƴi der fedde e jonde goɗɗo goɗɗo, faamu e laakal ngoni waawi ummaade.
Ngam majjum, kuugal fedde ngam foolde heende fuu, waawi arde e laawol keso nyaande hakkilantaagal ngam heedorde haaje gollordo.
Ko adii организации feeree waawde fedde jibinɗe, ardungal foti tagde aada jibinannde e bayyinaare ganndal e anndal fedde kadi.
Angel (2006) na himi seedi, o fahe anniya Continuum bana laawol ngol aadee yamiri waɗugo ngam wallita fedde be yotto daraja toowunde nder golle maɓɓe.
Bayyaneeki neurobiology ngal addi daliila jikkowaaɗo ngam laabiiji miijooji dow andal. Sabu ɗum, ɗum naftinaa nokkuure cuuɗugol e ɗum waɗi ɗum laaɓtungal no feewi.
Jonnde hakkunde nyaw e hakkilo e dabi'uuji walli janangooɓe nder njoftal mum en.
Ko ɗum anndaa ko juutiɗɗum wonde mboniiji garawal to bannge goɗɗe, raɗɗi, kuuje saɗɗe, e buubuuje mbaɗata ɗabi'uuji e ngonaa waylitorde e kuugal hakkiliji goɗɗe.
Ɓennugo teknolojiiye kesi'en na jeyna en miijo e deedugal nguurndam hakkille e golle hakkille ɗe nguurndam ngalaa yeeso.
Ɗum woni ko addana ɗemngal men habaruuji keewɗi e material ngam mahugo misalaaji, dii ngona wallude men faamude golle nder hakkillaaji amen.
Hay so AI woodi tinndol famɗe famɗe science fiction, AI no waɗi leggal mawnge nder jannde komputa, e golle ɗe kaajal, anndal e waylitaare hakkilo nder mashin.
Ndaalndal nder AI naatii wallugo masinji ngam waɗugo golle ɗe poti e hakkillo.
Misalaaji ɗon jeyaa e laamugo, tinndingo e aada, mbaawka jaabaandu e nyoŋe e lannda e lamlameeji yimɓe, waato gane binndol e daande e yeeso.
Koode nooneeji ngoni feddeeje tawi ko bee kollita faabooji ngam taskitaaki lororde ngeendam.
Ndeen AI ​​sistema jonta ko heewi huutoreeɗe nder fannuuji jaŋde ceede, hakkileeji, injiniyariya e konu, bana no aadeeji maaɓe e nder komputaaji galleeji e softwareeji fijirɗe video.

Ndaa misal, hitaande kala, janngooɓe Bennet School nder North Carolina ɓe mbaɗata website dow yawdugol maɓɓe haa State Capital, hitaande kala website ɗon newitaama, amma taggooje arande ɗe njokkataa dow internet ngam laatoo deftere memoraaji.
Blogji kadi no wallita ɓeydude binndol janngooɓe. Ɗum ko janngooɓe fuɗɗotoo no feewi e blogji maɓɓe bee binndol caahu bee laamuɗe, nde woni yimɓe no njooɗi no waylita ɗum.
Gam boɗeeɓe janngooɓe ɓuri haɗugo fellere, binndiyoowo blog fuɗɗoto wullaago ngam moƴƴinde binndol ngam reenaade haɗere.
Walaa kadi, windugo blogji "na famɗina ɗalm'en faamu e hakkillo dow aduna ɗo e mariingeeje mum." Bu'e faaboore yidde jaŋtooɓe na foola ɗalm'en laatoo wayluɓe e ɗuuɗɓe faayida (Toto, 2004).
Bloging ko kayan aiki moƴƴoowo golle pamarɗe e gooto e gooto, e o tabbitini janngooɓe ɓeyda jannde maɓɓe haa ɓuri ñalawma jannde deeneeri.
Ndeer yeeso golle blogji nootiiɗe "inaa waawi semmbinde taalibaaɓe ngam wuurtaade ɓe keeraniiɓe e jaŋtoɓe; tawa ɓe noota ko ɓe nanii e internet, taalibaaɓe ina mbaawi tinndinde nokkuuji maɓɓe nder keerol binndiiji woɓɓe e kadi tinndinde miijooji maɓɓe dow kuuje tawtoraaɗe (Oravec, 2002).

In Fulfulde, you must choose the correct pronoun which sometimes dictates the verb conjugation. Here are a few possibilities: **Option 1: Addressing a single person (formal/respectful - using *on*):** Si tawii on resinii jangoole e galleeji jooɗorde on ngam hitaande 2020 ado feeñnugo ɓaawo, on mbaawi wonde e caɗeele. **Option 2: Addressing a single person (informal - using *a*):** Si tawii a resinii jangoole e galleeji jooɗorde maa ngam hitaande 2020 ado feeñnugo ɓaawo, a mbaawi wonde e caɗeele. **Option 3: Addressing multiple people (using *onon*):** Si tawii onon resinii jangoole e galleeji jooɗorde mon ngam hitaande 2020 ado feeñnugo ɓaawo, onon mbaawi wonde e caɗeele. **Explanation of Choices:** * **Si tawii:** If * **on/a/onon resinii:** You (formal singular/informal singular/plural) booked. The verb *resinugo* (to reserve, to book) agrees with the pronoun. * **jangoole:** flights * **e galleeji jooɗorde:** and accommodation (literally: houses of staying) * **ngam hitaande 2020:** for the year 2020 * **ado feeñnugo ɓaawo:** before the postponement was announced (literally: before the lateness appeared/became known) * **on/a/onon mbaawi wonde:** You (formal singular/informal singular/plural) may be. The verb *wonde* (to be) is in the potential/subjunctive mood. * **e caɗeele:** in a difficult situation (literally: in difficulties) **I recommend using one of these translations depending on whom you are talking to. Ammaa sabu a joodinaama nder "luumooji nguleeki" seeda ɗuuɓi ɗiɗi haa woyla ekwetor, aɗa waawi haɓaade e nguleeki (hakkilla o tum tum) e naange tiiɗɗum (to kammu laaɓi, seeɗa ɓuri).
Haa jooni, woodi bisaji pamariɗɗi jahirowi to woyla haa Hebron, wuro ɗaanduujo maaɓe baba'en kitaabuji Ibrahima, Isiyaku, Yakubu, e rewɓe maɓɓe.
Ndaaru to bus a miijitoowo jogaade yilla Hebron, wata a yilla ɗo juulirɗe Yahuudiyanko'en Kiryat Arba ɓadi.
Laawol ndiyam nder leydi fotai weltaare nguurndam holla ko waawi wonde jaati nguurndam sawru.
Misal, yillaade gelleeji laamu nder Daande Loire, Daande Rhine, walla yahugo laana ngam yahaade gelleeji seedaniiɗi nder Danube, walla waalugo laana haa laawol Erie.
Ɓe keɓaa kadi laawol ngam laawuji yahirde e piindiɗe caakake ɗeɗɗe.
Jolal Kirsimas ko go'o nder jolli ɓurɗi teeŋtude nder diina Kiristaankeejum, e jollel nguurndam Yeesu Almasiihu.
Aadaaji keewɗi e dow jaɓɓorgal ngal, non-goonɗinɓe nder lesɗe Kiristaanko'en e non-Kiristaanko'en e adunaaru fuu ngiɗi ɗum.
Aadaaji ɗon ngoodi, a reenaa leydi naange ngam yeeso fuɗɗorde naange nder jemma Iista.
Ko non, tafsiirde janngirde diina Kiristaanko'en ngoodi ngam aada ɗum, amma wollaa ɗum waawan wonde aada tappere bee ribbinde nguurndam ko adii Kiristaanko'en.
Nder juulirde jamanuujo ɓuri, ɓe nasta juulde Easter Vigil hannde Asabarre kiikide nder Easter weekend, e jama'aare ɗon fe'a kaarɗe ngam seyinaa ummitaare Almasiihu nde yimɓe ɗuuɗi mbaɗata mawninkeejo e hakkunde jemma.
Dabbaaje denndaangal ɗe ardii ɗe ngari e duule ɗee ngarii ɗoo ko bee weeyde, bee fiyoowo, walla bee lumbal.
Sababtoo yeeso worgo hakkunde leydeendi, dabbaji nguurndam ngalaa haalarde yahugo, ngam dooɗeeri mawɗi laatii dabba kippanoowo arande nder Galapagos.
Gilla nde neɗɗo ari Galapagos, dabbaji pamarii ɗuuɗi ngarii, haa cikka bee ngeelooji, pucci, nagge, ɓiɓɓe, njawdi, haa bee rawaandu.
Si a yahi nokkuure Arctic bee Antarctic nder ndungu, a meeɗanayi leeso ooruki, ɗum woni naange fuuyaa e dow leydi.
Ɗum na'i dama laaɓunde ngam yeeso junngooji leeso (Aurora borealis), sabo kammu naniiɗum leeso waawi ɗun haa jemma fuu.
Ngam nokkuure ɗe jeyaaɗe ɗuuɗaani yimɓe, eɗum waawi laataade sonnere lemtagal annuraa’u ko ɗuum waɗi, aɗa waawi kadi welde yeeso hooreejam.
Aada golle Jappaaɓe ɓuri teddungal e laabiiji dow e nder kuugal ɓuri no aadeeji hirnaange janngintee.
Limse ko al'aada golle, bandiraaɓe golle noddirata hakkunde maɓɓe innde galleeji maɓɓe maa tittle golle maɓɓe.
Jam e golle ɗum muhimu sanne, ɗum tabbitini golle jama'a de walaa yettere haala gooto.
Golluɓe sey ko buri heddiiɓe maɓɓe jaɓi go'o fuu ɓe mbaɗi, e ɓe teeteerama ɓe ngoonɗina yamirooje buriɓe heddiiɓe maɓɓe ɗen, tawa na'i e haala.
